				<div class="post-media">

				<header class="post-header">

			 		<div class="post-categories"><a href="https://passionateaboutbaking.com/category/dessert/" rel="category tag">DESSERTS</a>,&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="https://passionateaboutbaking.com/category/eggless/" rel="category tag">EGGLESS</a>,&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="https://passionateaboutbaking.com/category/dessert/tarts-pies/" rel="category tag">TARTS, PIES</a>,&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="https://passionateaboutbaking.com/category/vegetarian/" rel="category tag">VEGETARIAN</a> </div>
										<h2 class="post-title">
						<a href="https://passionateaboutbaking.com/lotus-biscoff-coffee-tart/">Lotus Biscoff Coffee Tart &#8230; delicious dessert for coffee lovers</a>
					</h2>
					
										<div class="post-meta clear-fix">

													<span class="post-date">2025/10/21</span>
												
						<span class="meta-sep">/</span>
						
						<a href="https://passionateaboutbaking.com/lotus-biscoff-coffee-tart/#respond" class="post-comments" >0 Comments</a>
					</div>
					
				</header>

				
				<div class="post-content">
					<p>Biscoff Coffee Tart... just the simplest and most delicious dessert if your favourite flavour in the whole world is coffee AND if you love Biscoff, then you are in for a real treat since this eggless, no bake tart ticks off all the right boxes!</p>				</div>

				return;
			}
			if ( dropdown.value && parseInt( dropdown.value ) > 0 && dropdown instanceof HTMLSelectElement ) {
				dropdown.parentElement.submit();
			}
		}, 250 );
	}
	function onKeyUp( event ) {
		if ( 'Escape' === event.key ) {
			dropdown.dataset.lastkey = 'escape';
		} else {
			delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
		}
	}
	function onClick() {
		delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
	}
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'keyup', onKeyUp );
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'click', onClick );
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'change', onSelectChange );
})( "cat" );

//# sourceURL=WP_Widget_Categories%3A%3Awidget
/* ]]> */
</script>

			<script type="text/javascript">
/* <![CDATA[ */

( ( dropdownId ) => {
	const dropdown = document.getElementById( dropdownId );
	function onSelectChange() {
		setTimeout( () => {
			if ( 'escape' === dropdown.dataset.lastkey ) {
				return;
			}
			if ( dropdown.value ) {
				document.location.href = dropdown.value;
			}
		}, 250 );
	}
	function onKeyUp( event ) {
		if ( 'Escape' === event.key ) {
			dropdown.dataset.lastkey = 'escape';
		} else {
			delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
		}
	}
	function onClick() {
		delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
	}
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'keyup', onKeyUp );
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'click', onClick );
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'change', onSelectChange );
})( "archives-dropdown-8" );

//# sourceURL=WP_Widget_Archives%3A%3Awidget
/* ]]> */
</script>
